RSR_red_uprisings = {
	RSR_uprising_in_state_213 = {
		icon = generic_civil_support
		available = { has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 79 } }
		visible = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = RUS
				original_tag = VLG
			}
			213 = {
				NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT }
				CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { has_state_flag = red_rebels_called }
				OR = {
					any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_controlled_by = ROOT }
					any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no NOT = { state = PREV } is_controlled_by = ROOT } }
					AND = {
						ROOT = {
							OR = {
								has_completed_focus = VLG_attraction_of_peasant_leaders
								has_completed_focus = RUS_attraction_of_peasant_leaders
							}
						}
						OR = {
							any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no NOT = { state = PREV } any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no NOT = { state = PREV } is_controlled_by = ROOT } } }
							any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no NOT = { state = PREV } any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no NOT = { state = PREV } any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no NOT = { state = PREV } is_controlled_by = ROOT } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						is_coastal = yes
						OR = {
							any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes NOT = { state = PREV } is_controlled_by = ROOT } }
							any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes NOT = { state = PREV } any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes NOT = { state = PREV } is_controlled_by = ROOT } } }
							AND = {
								ROOT = {
									OR = {
										has_completed_focus = VLG_attraction_of_peasant_leaders
										has_completed_focus = RUS_attraction_of_peasant_leaders
									}
								}
								OR = {
									any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes NOT = { state = PREV } any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes NOT = { state = PREV } is_controlled_by = ROOT } } }
									any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes NOT = { state = PREV } any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes NOT = { state = PREV } any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes NOT = { state = PREV } is_controlled_by = ROOT } } } }
									any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes NOT = { state = PREV } any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes NOT = { state = PREV } any_neighbor_state = { impassable = no is_coastal = yes NOT = { state = PREV } is_controlled_by = ROOT } } } } }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > 14
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_CP_15
		days_remove = 14
		highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets = { state = 213 } }
		
		ai_will_do = { factor = 1 modifier = { add = 10 divisions_in_state = { size < 2 state = 213 } } modifier = { add = 100 divisions_in_state = { size < 1 state = 213 } } }
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -15 }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = RSR_red_uprising_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				create_template_Povstantsy = yes
				213 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT }
							ROOT = {
								OR = {
									has_completed_focus = VLG_attraction_of_peasant_leaders
									has_completed_focus = RUS_attraction_of_peasant_leaders
								}
							}
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Povstantsy\" division_template = \"Povstantsy\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 1" count = 2 allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
							owner = ROOT
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT } }
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Povstantsy\" division_template = \"Povstantsy\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 1" count = 2 allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
							owner = ROOT
						}
						set_state_flag = { flag = red_rebels_called days = 364 }
						ROOT = {
							add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
								type = infantry_equipment
								amount = -80
							}
						}
						else = { ROOT = { add_command_power = 15 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
